%% Diff

% Define commands for highlighting
% diff
\usepackage[most]{tcolorbox} % for boxes with transparency
% Define colors with transparency (opacity value)
\definecolor{GreenBG}{rgb}{0,1,0}
\definecolor{RedBG}{rgb}{1,0,0}
% Define tcolorbox environments for highlighting
\newtcbox{\greenhighlight}[1][]{%
  on line,
  colframe=GreenBG,
  colback=GreenBG!50!white, % 50% transparent green
  boxrule=0pt,
  arc=0pt,
  boxsep=0pt,
  left=1pt,
  right=1pt,
  top=2pt,
  bottom=2pt,
  tcbox raise base
}
\newtcbox{\redhighlight}[1][]{%
  on line,
  colframe=RedBG,
  colback=RedBG!50!white, % 50% transparent red
  boxrule=0pt,
  arc=0pt,
  boxsep=0pt,
  left=1pt,
  right=1pt,
  top=2pt,
  bottom=2pt,
  tcbox raise base
}

\begin{document}


%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%% Frontmatter
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\begin{frontmatter}
\begin{highlights}
\pdfbookmark[1]{Highlights}{highlights}

\item Neural trajectories in the hippocampus exhibited greater variability during a working memory (WM) task compared to those in the entorhinal cortex and amygdala regions.

\item The distance of neural trajectories between encoding and retrieval states in the hippocampus was memory-load dependent during a WM task.


\item Hippocampal neural trajectories fluctuated between the encoding and retrieval states in a task-dependent manner during both baseline and sharp-wave ripple (SWR) periods.

\item Hippocampal neural trajectories shifted from encoding to retrieval states during SWR period.

\end{highlights}\title{
Hippocampal neural fluctuations between memory encoding and retrieval states during a working memory task in humans
\DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{: Encoding-to-retrieval shift during sharp-wave ripples
}\DIFdelend }\author[1]{Yusuke Watanabe\corref{cor1}}
\author[2,3,4]{Yuji Ikegaya}
\author[1,5]{Takufumi Yanagisawa}

\address[1]{Institute for Advanced Cocreation studies, Osaka University, 2-2 Yamadaoka, Suita, 565-0871, Osaka, Japan}
\address[2]{Graduate School of Pharmaceutical Sciences, The University of Tokyo, 7-3-1 Hongo, Tokyo, 113-0033, Japan}
\address[3]{Institute for AI and Beyond, The University of Tokyo, 7-3-1 Hongo, Tokyo, 113-0033, Japan}
\address[4]{Center for Information and Neural Networks, National Institute of Information and Communications Technology, 1-4 Yamadaoka, Suita City, 565-0871, Osaka, Japan}
\address[5]{Department of Neurosurgery, Osaka University Graduate School of Medicine, 2-2 Yamadaoka, Osaka, 565-0871, Japan}

\cortext[cor1]{Corresponding author. Tel: +81-6-6879-3652}%%Graphical abstract

\begin{abstract}
\pdfbookmark[1]{Abstract}{abstract}

\section{Introduction}
Working memory (WM) \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{plays a }%%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{crucial role in everyday life, yet its underlying neural mechanisms remain to be fully elucidated}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{critical role in our daily activities, but the neural mechanisms underlying it are not completely understood}\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{critical role in our daily activities, but the neural mechanisms underlying it are not completely understood}\DIFaddend %%%

%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{function of the }\DIFdelend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{is essential for various daily tasks, yet we still lack full comprehension of the associated neural mechanisms. In particular, the }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{is essential for various daily tasks, yet we still lack full comprehension of the associated neural mechanisms. In particular, the }\DIFaddend hippocampus, a \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{key brain region involved in memory, warrants }\DIFaddend %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{crucial region for memory in the brain, demands continued }\DIFaddend investigation \cite{scoville_loss_1957,squire_legacy_2009,boran_persistent_2019,kaminski_persistently_2017,kornblith_persistent_2017,faraut_dataset_2018,borders_hippocampus_2022,li_functional_2023,dimakopoulos_information_2022}. \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\subsection{Calculation of neural trajectories using GPFA}
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{To }%%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{derive }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{extract }\DIFaddend %%%

%DIFDELCMD < \cite{yu_gaussian-process_2009} }\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
%DIFDELCMD < on the multiunit activity data for each session to extract }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{We utilized GPFA \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{yu_gaussian-process_2009} }\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD

%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{We implemented GPFA }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{GPFA was implemented }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{GPFA was implemented }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{. This was executed }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{. This was executed }\DIFaddend using the elephant package (\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{without }\DIFaddend overlaps. Each factor was z-normalized across all sessions. \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{The }\DIFaddend Euclidean distance from the origin ($O$) \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\subsection{Defining SWR candidates from hippocampal regions}
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{To pinpoint potential SWR events in the hippocampus, we used a detection method consistent with the consensus in the field \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \cite{liu_consensus_2022}}\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < . We re-referenced }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{A detection method in line with the field consensus \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \cite{liu_consensus_2022} }\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < was used to identify potential SWR events in the hippocampus. The }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{A detection method in line with the field consensus \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \cite{liu_consensus_2022} }\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < was used to identify potential SWR events in the hippocampus. The }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{To identify potential SWR events in the hippocampus, a widely accepted detection method was used \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
%DIFDELCMD < \cite{liu_consensus_2022}}\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
%DIFDELCMD < . The regional }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{To identify potential SWR events in the hippocampus, a widely accepted detection method was used \mbox{%DIFAUXCMD
\cite{liu_consensus_2022}}\hspace{0pt}%DIFAUXCMD
. The regional }\DIFaddend local field potential (LFP) signals\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{from a region of interest (ROI), such as AHL, }%%%

%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{, like those from AHL, were re-referenced }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{, like those from AHL, were re-referenced }\DIFaddend by subtracting the \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{average }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{mean }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{mean }\DIFaddend signal outside the \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{ROI }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{region of interest }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{region of interest }\DIFaddend (e.g., AHR, PHL, PHR, ECL, ECR, AL, AR) (see Figure~\ref{fig:01}A). \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{Using these }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{These }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{These }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{This }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{This }\DIFaddend re-referenced LFP signals \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{, we applied }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were used to apply }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were used to apply }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were used with }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were used with }\DIFaddend a ripple-band filter (80--140 Hz) \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{to }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{and }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{and }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdel{isolate }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{to discern the }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{to discern the }\DIFaddend SWR-positive (SWR$^+$) candidates (see Figure~\ref{fig:01}B). \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{We performed SWR detection }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{SWR detection was performed }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{SWR detection was performed }\DIFaddend %%%

%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{(}\DIFdelend %%%

\DIFdelend modifications such as a revised bandpass range of 80--140 Hz for human applications \cite{norman_hippocampal_2019,norman_hippocampal_2021} \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{over }\DIFaddend the original 150--250 Hz range \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{commonly used }\DIFaddend for rodents.

\indent
For SWR$^+$\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{candidates, }%%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{we defined }\DIFdelend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend %%%

\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{, the control events were defined as }\DIFaddend SWR-negative (SWR$^-$) \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{candidates }%%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were defined }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{were defined }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdel{as control events }\DIFdelend %%%
\DIFdelend by shuffling the timestamps of SWR$^+$ \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{candidates }\DIFdelend %%%

\subsection{Fluctuating hippocampal neural trajectories between encoding and retrieval states}
\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{Following this}\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{Subsequently}\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{Subsequently}\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdel{, we inspected }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{Subsequently, we examined }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{Subsequently, we examined }\DIFaddend the trajectory \textit{directions} based on $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$. Directions of SWRs were identified by the neural trajectory at $-250$ ms and $+250$ ms from their center (i.e., $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{eSWR^+}}$). \DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \\
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \indent
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdel{We }\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{From this data, we }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{From this data, we }\DIFaddend %%%
%DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{From these data, we }\DIFaddend %%%
\DIFdelend \DIFaddbegin \DIFadd{From these data, we }\DIFaddend computed the density of $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{eSWR}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$, $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{rSWR}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$, and $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{eSWR}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{rSWR}}$ (Figure 7A--D).\DIFdelbegin %DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdelbegin \DIFdel{$\overrightarrow{\mathrm{rSWR^-}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$ exhibited biphasic distributions.
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < }%%%
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \\
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \indent
%DIF < DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < %%%
%DIF < DIF < DIFDELCMD < \DIFdel{By comparing the distribution of $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{rSWR^+}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$ (Figures 7A \& B) with those of $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{rSWR^-}} \cdot \overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$ (Figures 7C \& D), we calculated the contributions of SWR (Figures 7E \& F), which unveiled a shift in the direction of $\overrightarrow{\mathrm{g_{E}g_{R}}}$ (Figures 7E \& F; see }%%%
